Deeply Concerned About the German Threat, France Actively Prepares Air Defense 36

High-Speed Bombers Capable of Traveling Between Berlin and Paris

Allocates 3.5 Billion French Francs to Improve Air Force

Paris - French Air Minister Denain attaches great importance to Germany's establishment of seaplane bases for air routes to South America. He gave a five-hour speech before the Aviation Committee of the Chamber of Deputies on this matter, stating that this plan is currently being discussed among the United Kingdom, France, and the United States, with the hope that the issue of opening international air routes between Europe and North America can be resolved in the near future. The original American initiator is also seeking patent rights, while the United Kingdom wants it to become an international undertaking. French aircraft manufacturer Blériot is paying close attention to this matter, hoping that a satisfactory solution can be reached among the three countries. The Air Minister also said that French pursuit aircraft will be developed to a high speed of 400 miles per hour, so that France's new bombers can carry a load of 1,000 kilograms and travel back and forth between Paris and Berlin. As for seaplanes, the situation in France is very unfavorable, and it is hard to compare with Italy, which has 2,000 new-style seaplanes. Therefore, France needs 3.5 billion French francs to improve its existing air force. Of the originally stipulated aviation expenditure of 900 million French francs, 500 million French francs have already been used. (National Telegram, 21st)

Paris - French Air Minister General Truant today refuted the alarming rumors that Germany has thousands of military aircraft before the Aviation Committee of the Chamber of Deputies, stating that Germany will have approximately 1,000 to 1,100 aircraft by the beginning of next year. The French Air Force is larger than Germany's, but its speed is slower and its equipment is not as new, so it is slightly inferior to Germany. If the French Air Force is completely reformed, it will cost approximately 330 million francs. The budget reporter will likely allocate 100 million francs from the supplementary national defense expenditures to the Air Force to make up for the inadequacy of regular expenses. (Reuters Dispatch, 22nd)

Paris - During today's hearing in the Chamber of Deputies, the Army Department expenditure reporter, Achard, made another alarming announcement regarding Germany's military position, stating that Germany's national defense budget expenditures have increased by 40% in the past two years. No previous German government has been as militaristic as the Hitler government. Germany has recently ordered aircraft engines from the United Kingdom and the United States, with a total value of several million British pounds. In addition, there are large orders to German specialized factories and new aircraft manufacturing plants. Achard then read out the French Army budget, requesting an allocation of 5,689,000,000 francs, not including the cost of border defense projects. In the morning, the French Army expenditure was 5,946,000,000 francs. (Reuters Dispatch, 21st)

League of Nations to Discuss Saar Issue Next Tuesday 37

French Foreign Minister Returns to Paris for a Trip

The Visit to Rome Extended to Next Year

Geneva - The Council of the League of Nations has scheduled a special meeting for November 27th to discuss the Saar plebiscite. French Foreign Minister Laval will attend this meeting. (Reuters Dispatch, 22nd)

Geneva - French Foreign Minister Laval, British Minister Eden, and Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov dined together today to discuss disarmament issues. Laval will return to Paris tomorrow evening and will not return to Geneva until next Monday, as the Saar issue cannot be discussed until that day. Mr. Alcidi, Chairman of the Saar Commission, also hopes to arrive here on Sunday. Laval expressed optimism about Franco-Italian relations, so he hopes to make the trip to Rome soon. The French side believes that Laval must wait until after the Saar region vote concludes in January of next year before he can proceed. (National Telegram, 21st)

Mineral Issue: France and Germany Reach Agreement in Principle 38

Laval's Diplomacy Criticized Domestically

Rome - Today, French and German experts are meeting here, and it is believed that they have reached an important agreement in principle regarding the mineral resources of the Saar region. They are currently discussing how Germany should compensate France if the plebiscite to be held next year favors the Saar's return to Germany. The amount of compensation will be discussed after experts from both countries arrive here tomorrow. According to a Reuters dispatch from Paris, it is widely believed that the agreement in principle reached by the French and German experts is based on the suggestion that Germany can purchase the mines using the French paper currency currently circulating in the Saar region. (Reuters, 22nd)

Geneva - The Saar Committee of the League of Nations has submitted a report to the Secretariat, reporting on its work in September and October. As of September 26, the number of registered voters was 532,740, of whom 59,794 resided outside the Saar region. The report also stated that the Committee has learned that a majority of local groups are very sympathetic to the German vanguard groups.

Paris - The diplomatic correspondent of the Parisian newspaper "Echo de Paris" criticized Foreign Minister Laval, saying that his handling of the Saar issue was too weak. Because Laval's methods are slow and indecisive, he has only caused disputes in the diplomatic arena. The newspaper previously criticized the late Foreign Minister Barthou severely, criticizing him for being too straightforward. Now, Laval has failed to fully follow Barthou's Saar memorandum, and except for taking a firm stance on economic issues, he has little initiative in other areas. The idea of holding another vote in ten years has now been abandoned. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Speech by Russian Representative at the Disarmament Conference 39

Arms Transport Should Also Be Subject to Control

Reiterating the Establishment of a Permanent Peace Organization

Geneva - Soviet People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs, Litvinov, delivered a speech at the plenary session of the Disarmament Conference here. Litvinov stated that the reason for the stagnation of the Disarmament Conference's work is that all countries, large and small, have failed to agree to fulfill various restrictions and obligations on disarmament. At the same time, this situation still exists today, so although the resolutions proposed by Henderson are valid, it is impossible to adopt them with limitations. Furthermore, regarding the issue of arms sales and manufacturing submitted by Henderson for discussion, Litvinov stated that the Soviet representative does not oppose it, because the Soviet Union does not have private arms sales or manufacturing. Therefore, this restriction has already taken effect in the Soviet Union, and he hopes that other countries can do the same. At this point, Litvinov suggested that the announcement of information should not be limited to the sale and manufacture of arms, but should also include the transport of arms. Henderson suggested forming a standing committee for disarmament. Litvinov believes that establishing it would be like "putting the cart before the horse," because this committee, no matter how eloquent, would be powerless in the near future. Therefore, adding it would be like legitimizing its inaction. The Soviet delegation then proposed forming a special organization with a broader mission and a permanent peace conference format, which would handle all issues related to creating security and peace guarantees. Therefore, Litvinov suggested that the plenary session should discuss Henderson's proposal to form a standing committee and the Soviet proposal for a permanent peace conference at the same time. Litvinov stated that if Henderson could agree to this point, he could withdraw his opposition to Henderson's proposal. (TASS, 21st)

Yugoslavia's Application to the League of Nations 40

Changing to a Formal Letter Under Pressure from Britain and France

Geneva - According to reliable French sources, Yugoslavia's application to the League of Nations, with the assistance of the foreign ministers of Romania and Czechoslovakia, is now planned to be changed to a formal letter to be submitted to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, requesting that the Marseille assassination case be included on the agenda of the regular meeting in January next year. Yugoslavia's change of the application to a formal letter this time is reportedly the result of pressure from Britain and France. Therefore, the memorandum will not be published this week and must be postponed until January next year. (National Telegram, 21st)

Geneva - The application submitted by the Yugoslav government to the League of Nations regarding the political responsibility for the Marseille assassination case has been jointly discussed by the foreign ministers of the Little Entente countries. The foreign ministers of the three countries have completely consistent opinions on the content and form of the application. This has been confirmed by the Yugoslav representative attending the League of Nations meeting. Yugoslav Foreign Minister Jevtic will likely submit the application to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol this afternoon. The full text of the application will be published in the evening. As for the governments of Romania and Czechoslovakia, they will notify the Secretariat of the League of Nations tomorrow, supporting Yugoslavia's application. In addition, the Yugoslav government will collect various documents to confirm the application and draft a memorandum, which will be published on Saturday this week or Monday next week. (Havas, 22nd)

Shi Zhichuan Arrives in Tokyo to Investigate the Judicial System 42

Tokyo - Shi Zhichuan, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Judicial Administration of the National Government's Executive Yuan, and Hong Wenlan, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Ministry, arrived in Tokyo yesterday, the 21st. On the 22nd, they visited Justice Minister Ohara at the Ministry of Justice accompanied by Yang Yunlun, Secretary of the Chinese Embassy. They briefly stated that they had come to Japan to investigate the actual situation of the judicial system for the purpose of reforming the judicial system for reference. They requested assistance and said that they planned to stay in Tokyo for a month and asked for permission to visit the actual conditions of various courts. The Justice Minister replied that he sincerely welcomed their arrival and asked them not to be polite and to fully inspect the situation. He also said that the Japanese Ministry of Justice would also make every effort to promote the improvement of the judicial system in their country. Shi and others also visited Vice Minister Kanesan, President Kazuhito of the Great Court of Cassation, and the six chief prosecutors of the court, including Chief Prosecutor Hayashi, and briefly stated their intentions. Full Text of the Indian Constitutional Reform Report 44

Advocating the Establishment of a Federal Government to Replace Centralization

Defense, Diplomacy, Finance, and Banking Still in the Hands of the Viceroy

Great Impact on the British Empire and Relations with the Far East

Will Trigger New Developments and Combinations East of Suez

London - The Indian constitutional reform report published by the Joint Committee today is the most important document in the history of the British Empire. Its suggestions may lead to future autonomy for the Indian government. The report advocates the immediate establishment of an All-India Federal Government consisting of eleven provinces and several departments to replace the current centralized government. However, several important issues related to the lifeline of India, such as finance, defense, and diplomacy, will still be under the jurisdiction of the Indian Viceroy. Most observers believe that this is the greatest freedom that Indians have long opposed British rule and is the beginning of establishing an autonomous government in India in the shortest period of time. What impact this move will have on the relationship between the Empire and the Far East is still unpredictable, but it is generally believed that its impact will be significant and may trigger new developments and combinations east of Suez. (National Telegram, 21st)

London - The content of the Indian constitutional reform Joint Committee's report, which is eagerly awaited by the general public, was released this afternoon. This move marks the completion of the most difficult task of studying and revising the constitution in the history of the British Empire or even the world.

The report advocates replacing the current centralized government system with an All-India federal system including autonomous units. The eleven provinces of India belonging to Britain (two of which will be newly created) and the princely states of India will form a federal system. The princely states will join the federation voluntarily. The internal administrative system of the princely states and the relationship between the princes and monarchs outside the scope of the federation will not be changed. However, the provinces will govern their own affairs on a larger scale than at present. Most of the administrative departments involving individuals, including laws, security, and certain taxes, will be the responsibility of the provinces. The federal government will manage matters related to the entire Indian body, such as currency and tariffs. Defense and foreign affairs will still be the direct responsibility of the Viceroy. Each province will have a legislative council, which will be elected by direct suffrage. Voters account for about 14 percent of the population. Five provinces will have both upper and lower houses. The federal government will have both upper and lower houses, which will be composed of those indirectly elected by the provinces and those designated by the princely states. The federal and provincial parliaments will both stipulate seats for various ethnic minorities. The executives of the federal and provincial governments are responsible to the parliaments, which is the same as the system in which the British cabinet is responsible to the parliament.

London - The Indian constitutional reform Joint Committee's report also advocates that the Governor-General and provincial governors should adopt the opinions of the cabinet members when their opinions do not conflict with certain special responsibilities entrusted to them by the constitution. The scope of responsibility of the Governor-General and provincial governors is quite broad, such as preventing harm to peace and security and protecting ethnic minorities, all of which are within their responsibility, and the Governor-General is also responsible for ensuring financial stability and credit. The report pays special attention to the issue of terrorism and makes special proposals. The federal and provincial governments should have a parliamentary government system unless the environment requires the Governor-General or provincial governor to exercise their special powers. The report advocates that Indian civil and police personnel must be recruited in Britain and proposes measures for police protection and discipline, and measures to ensure judicial independence from political influence. The report also has protective measures for British trade to prevent India from using its economic freedom to harm British trade through tariffs. The report finally recommends separating Burma from India and having the same constitution. The majority of the committee members agreed with the report. In the final vote, only three Conservative Party members, one Labour Party member in the upper house, and three Labour Party members and two Conservative Party members in the lower house expressed disagreement. The report of the committee is slightly different from the White Paper in terms of safeguards, such as any legislation concerning police discipline must be agreed to by the provincial governor, and reports on the activities of terrorist parties must be instructed by the provincial governor and must not be announced to outsiders. The provincial governor has the power to accept any administrative department in order to eliminate terrorist acts. Madras, Bombay, Bengal, the United Provinces, and Bihar will establish upper houses. The Indian legislature will have the right to petition for amendments to the constitution concerning the organization of parliament and suffrage ten years later. After the separation of Burma and India, a separate commercial treaty will be established. As for the appointment of judges, it will be in the charge of the High Court. (Reuters, 21st)

British Parliament Will Conduct Detailed Research and Begin Debate Before Christmas 45

London - British Prime Minister MacDonald moved in the House of Commons that the time of all members of parliament during this session must be used to discuss the report of the Indian constitutional reform committee and the Indian bill to be proposed by the government. Today, the House of Commons passed this motion by a vote of 224 to 62. The Prime Minister said that the Indian bill contains 300 articles and the government will spend most of its time on this. The debate on the report will be held before Christmas, and the second reading of the Indian bill will be held after Christmas and before Easter. From Easter to the end of July, most of the parliamentary time will be used for detailed discussion of various articles of the Indian bill. The Labour Party members of the Joint Committee submitted another report, advocating that the structure of the new Indian constitution should enable India to achieve the status of overseas autonomous territory through internal development procedures, without the need to request approval from the British Parliament again. It also said that safeguards are necessary, but they should be for the purpose of protecting the people from being abused. The Labour Party members expressed serious opposition to the establishment of the two houses of the legislature, saying that the provinces of India may well be allowed to try it according to the Westminster system, but the central responsibility should be exercised by a committee of the legislature composed according to the Ceylon constitution. There should only be one central legislature, in which the Labour Party should have 26 seats, and the Governor-General should not have the special responsibility of ensuring financial stability and credit. Ford of the Liberal Party expressed the Liberal Party's views on this report, saying that the Liberal Party representatives who participated in this committee opposed the election of the lower house of the central legislature from a direct system to an indirect system, fearing that this change would greatly disappoint the Indian people. But in general, the Liberal Party representatives agreed with the report's proposals, and the Liberal Party in the House of Commons and the country will definitely support this case, as it is a great advance in the autonomy of India. (Reuters, 21st)

London - The draft reform of the Indian constitution proposed by the government will be studied by a joint committee of the two houses. After 18 months of work, the committee has completed the report, which was released this afternoon. This document is of great importance to the future of the British Empire. Its content fully recognizes the government's draft, but puts forward three reservations, which are directly in line with the views expressed by those who criticize the government's draft. The points reserved in the report are: 1. All laws concerning police power must obtain the consent of the provincial governors before they are implemented, and the provincial governors are the representatives of the King of England. 2. Whenever it is necessary to suppress terrorism, the Indian government has full power to supervise any part of the administrative affairs. 3. It is firmly advocated that the Governor-General of India has the power of veto if it is proposed to tax goods transported from the UK mainland to India. The above three items are the main reservations, known as safeguard clauses, which the Conservative Party wants to include in the constitution. With the committee's report in hand, it is easy to understand the content of the government's draft and engage in research. Parliament's discussion of the government's draft will be carried out in three stages and will last for about five months. After the draft is passed in principle, a line-by-line discussion will begin. At least the last few months of this session will be devoted to line-by-line discussion. It can be seen from this that the UK and public opinion attach great importance to the reform of the Indian constitution. All members of parliament regard India as a symbol of the prosperity of the British Empire. (Havas, 21st)

Covering Up People's Eyes and Ears to Hinder Autonomy, Indian Public Opinion Expresses Great Dissatisfaction 46

New Delhi - Indian public opinion on the report of the Indian Constitutional Reform Committee has condemned the committee for failing to adopt the concept of autonomy in overseas territories, and pointed out that the constitutional provisions it has drafted are harsh and difficult to develop. However, with the exception of the extreme faction of the National Congress, all political parties understand the need to use their acquired powers to promote social and economic progress by proposing legislation in accordance with constitutional procedures. It is generally believed that this report exposes the weaknesses of the constitution, especially the two-headed political system in the center. It is generally said that this system will prevent the development of genuine and spontaneous cooperation between the British and Indian peoples. The Indian National Congress agency Minsheng (民聲) claimed that the fear of the Indian Liberal Party that the mixed committee would be subdued by the radical faction in Britain has now been proven to be correct. The rare shadow of responsibility contained in the White Paper is now becoming increasingly illusory due to the retrograde proposals in the report. In fact, it is just shelving the Indian issue. The Indian people now hope that the British Labour Party will take power so that this constitution can be amended as soon as possible. Sapru, a Liberal Party member of the Indian Executive Council, told a Reuters interviewer that the reforms proposed in the report have failed to satisfy any aspect of public sentiment. The British Liberal Party had proposed a plan for direct elections in the center, but it was rejected, causing the original plan in the White Paper to lose its only advantage of being able to influence the people. The proposed reform plan has abolished the central democracy system and is only a move to cover up people's eyes and ears. It not only wants to consolidate the existing interests of Britain, but also wants to hinder progress towards autonomy. (Reuters, 20th)

Verdict on the Japanese Blood Pledge Corps Case 47

Inoue and Three Others Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Furuuchi and Eleven Others Sentenced to Imprisonment

Tokyo - Inoue Nissho's Blood Pledge Assassination Corps, composed of fourteen comrades, advocated "one person, one kill" and assassinated privileged class, party, zaibatsu, and famous figures in order to establish the Showa Restoration. In February of the year before last, they assassinated former Minister of Finance Inoue Junnosuke and Mitsui zaibatsu representative Dan Takuma, etc., inducing the sensational May 15th Incident. After the Metropolitan Police Department arrested the party members, the judicial authorities conducted the trial. In the twelfth public trial, the presiding judge, Coconut Breaking Tribunal, was replaced by Fujii as the presiding judge, and the trial was started by two judges, Kyomori and Ino, and two prosecutors, Kinouchi and Kishimoto. It is reported that the public trial reached 91 times before and after. On the morning of the 22nd, at 2:20, the verdict was announced at the Tokyo District Court as follows:

(The sentences sought by the prosecutors are in parentheses)

Furuuchi Eiji - 15 years imprisonment (Death Penalty)

The police stationed at the station were outnumbered and all their weapons were confiscated by the bandits. Ten police officers and staff were abducted by the bandits. International Commercial Telegraph

—Special Business Report from Reuters on November 22nd— 102

Gold and Silver

London: The gold price today was quoted at a low of 3 pence and a half.

London: The spot silver price today was 24 pence 5625, and the futures price was 24 pence 6875, both up 125. The market is stable, with purchases from India and speculators, while China is buying and selling.

Mumbai: The silver market today was stable. The spot closing price was 66 rupees and 15 annas, up 4 annas.

Montreal: The silver market opened without movement, with an upward trend.

Exchange Rates

This morning, the British pound showed a slight improvement against the US dollar. Otherwise, the London foreign exchange market was quiet and uninteresting, with minimal fluctuations. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was 4 dollars 99 and a half cents, the same as yesterday's closing rate. Before noon, the British pound fell by 125 to 4 dollars 99 and 375 cents, and there were no further changes.

Decline in Japanese Agricultural Harvest 106

Unprecedented Disaster in a Decade

National Harvest of Fifty Million Koku

The natural disasters in Japan this year have been extremely severe and have spread throughout the entire country. The drought in Kyushu is already serious enough to put the local rural areas in a very difficult situation. The windstorms in Osaka, Kobe, Hyogo Prefecture, and Kyoto Prefecture, while not fatal blows, were not minor injuries. The frost damage in the northeastern prefectures of Aomori, Fukushima, Yamagata, Miyagi, Akita, and Iwate is particularly severe, transforming a relatively modern rural area into a state before the Middle Ages. The sale of daughters is almost an open transaction—said to be worth ten yen per year of age. The average farmer is in a state of malnutrition. In the rural areas of the northeastern prefectures, only two or three out of ten families have white rice to eat. The rest eat coarse grains, and the worst even chew on grass roots.

Moreover, the actual harvest is worse than generally expected, even worse than estimated by many agricultural experts. Since the initial estimate of 57 million koku of rice this year, the Kansai region has been hit by a major windstorm during the rice flowering season, resulting in significant losses. In addition, the climate in various regions has been very cold, unsuitable for the maturation of grains, further reducing the harvest. In fact, the harvest is 20.08 million koku less than last year (a decrease of approximately 28%), with the actual harvest only being 50.746 million koku. This is still an estimate and not a definitive figure based on actual facts.

Twenty years ago (1913), Japan experienced a major disaster, with a total national harvest of 50.259 million koku. At that time, the average harvest per tan (approximately 1.488 acres) was 1 koku 5 to 9 sheng 5 he. Before that, in the 43rd year of the Meiji era (1910), the average harvest per tan was 1 koku 5 to 8 sheng 1 he, which was the lowest recorded in Japan in recent decades. However, at that time, agricultural technology was not advanced, the grain varieties were poor, there were many shortcomings in cultivation, and fertilizer application was not optimal, so the harvest was naturally low. Recently, agricultural technology, while still in a handicraft state, has reached the highest level of handicraft. In particular, cultivation has been thoroughly improved, and major tasks such as fertilizer application and seed selection have made great progress. Furthermore, the area of cultivated land has also increased annually. From 1929 to last year, the average harvest for five years was 62.573 million koku. Compared to this year, the amount of the decrease is truly alarming.

In terms of the situation in each region, using the average figures for the past five years as a standard, Hokkaido has a decrease of 15.4%, the six northeastern prefectures affected by frost damage have a decrease of 40%, the seven Kanto prefectures have a decrease of 15%, the four Hokuriku prefectures have a decrease of 19%, the three Tosando prefectures have a decrease of 14.4%, the three Tokai prefectures have a decrease of 16.6%, the six Kinki prefectures have a decrease of 14.7%, the five Chugoku prefectures have a decrease of 11.4%, the four Shikoku prefectures have a decrease of 23.9%, and the seven Kyushu prefectures have a decrease of 18.2%. Only Okinawa Prefecture (the former Ryukyu Islands) has an increase of 53%. Among the six northeastern prefectures, Iwate Prefecture has the most severe decrease, accounting for 58.9%, making it the worst-harvesting area in Japan. Next is Aomori with a decrease of 46.7%, Yamagata with a decrease of 39%, Miyagi with a decrease of 38%, Fukushima with a decrease of 36.4%, and Akita with a decrease of 25%. Looking at this situation, Japan may be like the United States. Due to the reduction in the harvest, the general rural economy may actually improve significantly.

According to statistics from the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, there are currently more than 16.389 million koku of rice stored in Japan. Adding this year's 50.746 million koku and 13 million koku of imported rice, the consumption budget is only 71 million koku. Even after removing the estimated 5 million koku that is too high, there is still a surplus of 3.7 million koku. The reality is probably not as good, because among the 16.389 million koku currently stored, the government holds more than 11 million koku, which cannot be eaten freely by the people. Even if the Japanese government sells it to the people at a lower price, the effect of the transfer will still be limited, and the food shortage in the rural areas will remain severe. (Tokyo, November 14)

The Six Counties of Southern Jiangxi Are Designated as a Special District 107

—Implementing the "Three Chiefs" System to Teach, Nurture, and Defend—

Nanchang Dispatch: Ruijin, Shicheng, Yudu, Huichang, Xingguo, and Ningdu, six counties in southern Jiangxi, have been occupied by bandits for six or seven years, also known as the so-called Central District by the Red bandits. Except for Xu Huichang, which is still occupied by the remaining bandit forces, the rest have been recovered one after another. However, these six counties have been occupied by the bandits for a long time, and the red influence is deep. Social organizations and human relations have been completely overturned. Economic structures and production functions have also been almost completely destroyed. The people's minds have been anesthetized by the bandits, and their actions have been controlled by the bandits, all of which have become deeply ingrained and difficult to reverse. Therefore, for these six counties, special political means should be used to make urgent corrections, in order to eliminate the toxic bacteria, allow them to breathe and recuperate, and gradually restore their vitality to achieve restoration. Therefore, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specifically ordered the Jiangxi Provincial Government to designate these six counties as a special administrative region, devoting all its efforts to suppressing the remaining bandits, providing relief to the disaster-stricken people, and carrying out self-sufficiency and self-defense work. After receiving the order, Xiong Shihui, in consultation with the relevant departments, drafted the outline of the special district's administrative program, implementing the "Three Chiefs" system of principals, township heads, and Baojia heads as instructed by Chiang Kai-shek, focusing on education, nurturing, and defense. Principals promote special education to correct people's hearts; township heads manage rural economic organizations to provide a livelihood; and Baojia heads train the people to enable them to defend themselves. Then, they engage in construction to achieve the goal of restoration. Those who have already been put into practice include Xie Shouru, the magistrate of Xingguo County; Ma Yaoxiang, the magistrate of Ruijin County; Shao Hongji, the magistrate of Ningdu County; Li Yonghuai, the magistrate of Yudu County; and a certain county magistrate of Shicheng County, all of whom have taken office and are working. Wang Youlan and Shao Hongji, the special commissioners of the Tenth and Twelfth Districts, have also personally gone to Xingguo and Ningdu counties to work.

After returning to the province from inspecting Shicheng and Xingguo, Director Lü Min of the Civil Affairs Department will set off for Ruijin to supervise everything. Relief personnel from the preparation meeting place and the emergency relief shelter, as well as the medical and treatment teams providing medicine at the anti-epidemic office, are also departing one after another. More than ten sets of cotton clothing collected from various circles have been successively transported to Shicheng, Xingguo, and Ningdu for distribution. The Special Education Department of the General Headquarters has also established a special education promotion office for the six counties in Ningdu, appointing Wen Xingxiang as the director, and selecting 24 graduates from the second phase of special teacher training to go to various counties to run public schools. In addition to completing the Yongfeng to Gulonggang and Guangchang to Shicheng lines, the Highway Department also plans to complete the highway plan for the six counties, forming construction teams to set off for construction. (November 20)

Norlha Khutughtu Arrives in Hankou 108

Heading to Hunan to Preside Over a Prayer Ceremony for Peace

Hankou Dispatch: Norlha Khutughtu, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, accepted the invitation of He Jian, the head of Hunan, to go to Changsha to preside over a prayer ceremony for peace. He arrived in Hankou from Beijing on the 20th and stayed for several days. The threshold of those who went to worship was worn through. He often used chanting and stroking to cure people's illnesses. When the reporter visited, he was granted an audience and talked about his experiences in Kangding, maintaining the five-race republic, and escaping from prison in great detail. He also explained the differences between the Exoteric and Esoteric schools of Buddhism. The record is as follows:

The Bloody Battles in Western Sichuan: I was originally in Western Sichuan, named Zha Ka Lama, one of the great Living Buddhas of Western Sichuan. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, Zhao Erfeng, the Qing Dynasty's resident minister in Tibet, attacked the black sect rebels and suffered repeated defeats. Because the black sect followers harassed everywhere, I volunteered and quelled the rebellion in one fell swoop. Emperor Xuantong granted me the title of Grand Director-General. After the founding of the Republic of China, there was no strength to take care of the border areas. The Dalai Lama was tempted by the British to plot rebellion and destroy the five-race republic. I was the first to oppose it, which led to armed conflict. From the first to the sixth year of the Republic of China, we fought bloodily for six years. The Dalai Lama used British-style guns and cannons, and his strength was stronger. Peng Ersun, under the command of Chen Xialing, the garrison commander of the Sichuan border, had also defected. Our side had no way to call for help and gradually became unsustainable, leading to defeat and retreat. In the seventh year of the Republic of China, the Dalai Lama imprisoned me in a Tibetan prison. I managed to escape after several years.

Escaping from the Tibetan Prison: After escaping from the prison, I traveled at night and begged from door to door, receiving people's offerings. Later, I met a woman who donated a sheepskin coat, which saved me from hunger and cold. I safely escaped to India. Coincidentally, a woman had a strange disease, which I cured, and she gave me a thousand pounds of gold. Only then did I transfer to Hong Kong and take a ship north. It was in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China. Duan Qirui took power and sent a telegram inviting me to Beijing, where he supported me, giving me a monthly salary of a thousand yuan. Except for living expenses, I donated everything to charity. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, I went to Sichuan and stayed in Chongqing for four years, establishing the Sichuan-Kang Advancement Association. Recently, I went to Beijing.

Exoteric and Esoteric Buddhism: Buddhism has Exoteric and Esoteric schools. Generally speaking, the Exoteric school holds fasts and is vegetarian, while the red and yellow sects of the Esoteric school do not. In fact, holding fasts and being vegetarian is Taoism. Buddhist teachings only prohibit killing, and there is no prohibition on eating meat. Raising and eating meat is not killing. Moreover, according to Buddhist rules, monks can eat three kinds of pure meat: one, not seen; two, not heard; three, not suspected. Therefore, not eating meat is only a special prohibition, not a universal precept. On the contrary, those who study the highest Esoteric school consider not eating meat to be a violation of the precepts. Everyone can learn the Exoteric school, but the Esoteric school is more difficult. For example, Bodhicitta is the soil, the Exoteric school is the tree, and the Esoteric school is the fruit on the tree.

Treating Diseases Without Medicine: People's diseases are mostly caused by karmic retribution. I use my mind to generate compassionate thoughts, silently chant mantras, and then stroke the patient. Naturally, they can be cured without medicine. However, if the patient is not sincere, I am not sure. Performing empowerment and transmitting the Dharma is nothing more than eliminating disasters, resolving difficulties, and increasing wisdom. In particular, the Amitabha mantra and the Manjushri mantra have incredible effects.

Strange News of a Corpse Transformation in the Old Capital 109

Yan Yuting Dies for Twelve Days

Dead During the Day, Alive at Night, Breathes on People

Those Breathed On Often Become Half-Crazy

Beiping Dispatch: The saying of corpse transformation is seen in ancient books and unofficial history notes, described in great detail, as if it were indeed true. In recent years, as scientific knowledge has gradually reached the people, although the legends in rural areas still mix in tales of gods and ghosts, it is rarely found in metropolitan commercial ports. Unexpectedly, in the residence at No. 23 Bingmasi Lane, Nanluoguxiang, outside Di'anmen in the northern city of Beiping, there is a strange tale of corpse transformation, dead during the day and alive at night, spreading throughout the old city. The reporter went to investigate in person and recorded the situation witnessed as follows:

The deceased's name is Yan Yuting, 69 years old this year. He was a house manager in the residence of a high-ranking official, so he lived in leisure in his old age and was quite well-off. His son, Yongde, suffered from hemiplegia and all medicines were ineffective. Recently, he also developed phlegm congestion. Thirteen days ago (the 19th), he died of suffocation due to phlegm. He died in the morning. His family prepared a coffin and burial items. Unexpectedly, one day after Yan's death, at night, he suddenly opened his eyes, gasped, and spoke loudly. However, his tone was clearly not his own. At first, they suspected it was phlegm congestion, temporary shortness of breath, or that he had come back to life. However, Yan had died and was ice-cold, and his whole body was stiff, completely a dead corpse phenomenon. In terms of facts and experience, there was absolutely no reason for resurrection. Moreover, he spoke nonsense. After one night, at dawn, he suddenly lay on his back, stiff, ice-cold, and dead. At night, the same phenomenon as the first time was repeated. His son was helpless and prayed to the local land temple, which is the most superstitious in the lower class of society. When he returned home from the temple, he was also muttering to himself, like a neurotic, showing the same strange state as his father. The deceased's wife begged four strong men from her neighborhood to come to her house to keep watch at night. Unexpectedly, before the end of the night, these four men shouted and opened the door to escape. The corpse jumped up and wanted to get up, chasing after them madly, breathing on people they met. A certain old woman in a neighboring courtyard happened to be walking towards the corpse. After the corpse blew on her face, the old woman immediately went into a frenzy, using both hands to support the ground, making her feet stand upright in the air, like the martial artist's so-called "handstand." The neighbors in the same courtyard felt uneasy because Yan's family's corpse had turned mad. Counting that the corpse had been dead during the day and alive at night, continuously making noise, for thirteen days. Everyone was helpless, so they jointly reported it to the police station. Duan Wenxiu, the patrol officer of the 19th section of the 5th district, led the police to investigate. Indeed, they saw Yan's corpse still lying on the pit. Yue Zuomin, the household registration officer who came with him, used a flashlight to shine on the dead man's face. Unexpectedly, the dead man's eyes suddenly opened with it, and at the same time, he made a gesture to get up, and blew air towards the police officer's face. The police officers present were alarmed by this strange sight and were on guard. They reported to the Public Security Bureau. The Bureau has now notified the newspapers not to promote the gods and monsters claiming corpse transformation, and should consider it a residual state of dying from phlegm congestion and shortness of breath after not dying for many days. However, Yan Yuting has not yet officially died, and the strange phenomenon of being dead during the day and alive at night, with a cold and stiff body and speaking loudly, continues to be performed unabated. It is said that this matter is worthy of special study by scientists and the medical community. (19th)

Wuxi

Collection Fees for Land Tax Must Not Be Shared 113

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance believes that the collection fees for land tax in various counties should be entirely allocated to the expenses of the Land Tax Collection Office. The collection fees for deed tax and official document fees should be entirely allocated to the expenses of the Promotion Office and the Deed Tax Office. With fixed expenses in each of these offices, handling public affairs is easier, and the staff in each office can be allocated salaries, which can encourage honesty. However, it has recently been found that some counties are accustomed to old habits, often regarding collection fees as a special income, dividing and sharing them, putting them all into private pockets, which in turn causes the expenses of each office to be stripped away, and the salaries of the staff are not paid at all. This not only hinders the progress of public affairs, but also makes it impossible to prevent the staff from engaging in private malfeasance. This is a great loss to the original intention of the Department to rectify the collection methods in various counties. Yesterday, it specifically issued a notice to all counties, requiring that all the above-mentioned collection fees must be collected and allocated as much as possible, and allocated separately to the expenses of each office. The responsible personnel of each office should still prepare receipts for the amounts collected and allocated, and the county government should fill out expenditure vouchers and hand them over to the accounting director for registration and verification. In the future, if the amount collected is found to be inappropriate, it will be treated as private malfeasance, in order to clear up long-standing malpractices and maintain official integrity.

Chamber of Commerce Delegates City Merchants to Telegraph Condolences to the Soldiers Suppressing Bandits 123

This Victory Is Indeed an Opportunity to Revive the Nation's Foundation

The Failure to Achieve Final Victory Requires Continued Efforts in the Future

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed yesterday to express condolences to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and the soldiers of all armies suppressing bandits. The original text reads: "Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Nanchang Military Headquarters: The Red bandits have been rampant for seven years, and the Gan River basin has been poisoned almost everywhere. In addition, foreign troubles have taken advantage of the situation, and during the rampant period, they have almost grown out of control. The Central Plains was shocked. Your Excellency wielded the axe to lead the expedition, carefully planning in silence, not seeking immediate success, but focusing on changing accumulated habits and boosting morale. As a result, the defenses of Linhuai were completely renewed, the soldiers were dedicated, and the common people were pleased. Eventually, they were able to use more support to defeat less support, and the old nests of accumulated years were rescued. The people celebrated their revival. This is probably due to the divine calculations of Marquis Wu, who attacked the mind, and the fortunate diligence of the soldiers who fought a hundred battles, both of which combined to achieve this great achievement. Compared with the former Generals Li and Zeng, who supervised the army to suppress the Nian rebels, building long walls and clearing the people's villages, the effect of siege and encirclement was similar, but the efforts were even greater. The entire business community of Shanghai is grateful for Your Excellency and all the soldiers' hard work, and they are also celebrating that this victory is an opportunity to revive the nation's foundation, which was about to be destroyed. Therefore, they dare to send a telegram to express condolences to the soldiers and to show the gratitude of the people. If it is approved, please inform all the armies and share this intention. However, the remnants of the bandits have escaped, and a large-scale pursuit is required. The failure to achieve final victory requires continued efforts in the future. With Your Excellency's wisdom, there will be ways to comfort the people's hopes. With sincerity and dedication, we only ask for your consideration. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce kowtows."

Signing of the Huai River Grain Contract 128

More than Ten Purchasing Manufacturers

Transported by Dada Company

According to the Huadong News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, due to the Huai River Guidance Project, has specially entrusted the Jiangban Provincial Farmers' Bank to handle the transportation and sales of grain. The bank has signed a contract with the Shanghai grain industry and Dada Shipping Company is responsible for the transportation. The details are as follows:

Negotiation Process: Since the start of the Huai River Guidance Project, all workers' grain has been entrusted to the Jiangban Farmers' Bank for handling. The bank specifically ordered Hu Duming, the director of the transportation and sales office, to contact Gu Xinyi, the chairman of the Shanghai Grain Association. After several consultations, a contract has been signed. The grain ordered this time is 40% rice and 60% flour (No. 3 flour). The purchasing manufacturers include Huafeng, Shenda, and Leading Cengfeng, etc., more than ten in total. Each factory will extract one-thousandth of the flour they produce specifically for the workers of the Huai River Guidance Project. The term is six months and the price is temporarily set at one yuan and seven jiao to seven jiao and five fen.

Dalian is responsible for transporting all the flour by Dada Shipping Company. The factories deliver goods every other day, and the company transports about 2,000 packages a day to Qingjiangpu. Then, Zhou Hanxiang, the bank's special commissioner, is responsible for distributing them to Dongkan and Lianshui, two grain distribution stations, and then directly to the project site.

Purchasing Rice: A reporter from the Huadong News Agency learned from relevant sources that the project site believes that the workers are mostly from the north, so flour cannot suit everyone. Therefore, they have ordered another 40% of rice from the grain industry. The price of rice has been high recently, so a special commissioner has been sent to the interior to purchase it, and they will select purchases separately in Nanjing, Nantong, Suzhou, Wuxi, Qingjiangpu, and other places.

China Merchants Bureau's Second New Hai Ship, Hai Xiang, Expected to Arrive Tomorrow 129

Captain Appointed by a Chinese National

The China Merchants Bureau's second new Hai ship, Hai Xiang, left England on October 6th to be delivered in Shanghai. When the ship departed from Glasgow, Scotland, Ma Jiajun, Teng Shibiao, Zhang Guoquan, etc., who were sent by the Bureau to learn to drive and operate the ship's engine, returned to Shanghai with it. The representative of the shipyard, Marconi & Co., notified the China Merchants Bureau yesterday that the Hai Xiang passed Hong Kong on the 20th and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on the 24th (tomorrow). However, there has been fog on the sea these days, and the arrival time may be delayed. After the Hai Xiang arrives in Shanghai, it must enter the Jiangnan Factory for inspection before being officially accepted.

Successful Negotiation: Zhou Houkun, deputy director of the shipping department, was sent to Hong Kong by the Bureau when the first Hai ship, Hai Yuan, set sail, to request a new passenger license for the ship from the Hong Kong Shipping Administration Office and to negotiate for the captain of the Hai ship to be Chinese. It has been confirmed that the Hong Kong Shipping Administration Office, as a result of Mr. Zhou's negotiations, has issued the new passenger license and approved the Chinese to drive the Hai ship without examination, etc. Mr. Zhou has telegraphed his departure from Hong Kong to Shanghai.

Crew Appointed: The Bureau held a board meeting yesterday. Liu Hongsheng proposed that Ma Jiajun be appointed as the new captain of the Hai Xiang (the original owner of the Xin Ming ship, who went to England this time to learn to drive the new ship). The first mate is Sun Fuge, the second mate is Xu Dequ, and the third mate is Huang Jicheng. The engine chief is transferred from the Hai Xiang ship, Nelson. The first engineer is Li Yunmao, the second engineer is Wang Qingting, and the third engineer is Lu Guoshun. These appointments have been sent to the shipping department yesterday, and the crew will be notified tomorrow when the new ship arrives in Shanghai and after the ship's hull is inspected, they will go aboard to serve.

Special Features of the Machinery: The advantages of the machinery in the four new ships are not available in the other Hai ships, and are unique to these four ships. One is the freshwater manufacturing machine. In the past, commercial ships had to carry enough drinking water. If the freshwater supply was interrupted, they had to stop sailing to find it and then set sail again. Now, all four ships have freshwater manufacturing machines. Even if the water supply is cut off, seawater can be filtered and extracted for drinking at any time. Another is the water tank alarm. If the water tank overheats, the machine will explode immediately. Now the new ships have an alarm to report the water tank temperature and use fuses. Even if one part explodes, there is still a machine that can keep the ship sailing and avoid unexpected dangers. These are truly special features.

Wang Qingmu's Letter to Chairman Chen of Jiangsu on the Issue of Joint Governance of Chongming and Qidong 130

Mr. Wang Qingmu's letter to Chairman Chen of Jiangsu stated: "I came to the province yesterday to pay my respects, but you had already gone to Huaiyin to lead the commencement of the Huai River estuary project, bustling about and enduring hardships, which is admirable. I met with Secretary-General Luo, who indicated that the Civil Affairs Bureau had submitted a document opposing the joint governance of Chongming and Qidong. I suspect that the Civil Affairs Bureau does not fully understand the advantages and disadvantages of separation, or has listened to prior opinions and holds preconceived notions. One of these two must be the case. Otherwise, the people of Chongming and Qidong would not have sent legal representatives to petition for relief, claiming that they are suffering from the division. It is by no means a groundless complaint, so how can it be ignored? The public petition from Huang Housheng and others in Chongming stated that those who advocate separation aim to plunder property. This is the truth and cannot be concealed. Under the current accounting system, funds from category A cannot be used for category B, and funds from category C cannot be used for category D. The boundaries are clear. The Chongming seawall public land is a special fund for annual repairs, and the charity fund is a special fund for helping the orphaned and impoverished. Even if Qidong can be divided into a county, harming this to benefit that is not reasonable. Moreover, Qidong's acquisition of the seawall public land has not been used for seawall construction, and its acquisition of the charity fund has not been used for helping the orphaned and impoverished. It only causes significant losses to Chongming, while Qidong gains nothing. If the separation is not revoked, those who plunder Chongming's property will enjoy unwarranted rights and receive unexpected guarantees. How can this reversal of right and wrong be justified? Although the people of Chongming are weak, how can they not voice their grievances? Moreover, there are more unreasonable aspects of the separation than this. The outer sand of Chongming is cut off to form a county, but the tax quota originally borne by the outer sand is spread over the inner sand. The middle class is raised to the upper class, and the lower class is raised to the middle class, causing farmers to suddenly increase their suffering. This is the first unreasonable aspect. The county division violates public opinion, and Chongming's administrative expenses are insufficient, so it should request subsidies from the provincial treasury. However, it is forcibly imposing a surtax on land tax under the name of administrative subsidies. This is the second unreasonable aspect. Most of the land in Qidong belongs to the people of Chongming. All the people of Chongming have fulfilled their tax obligations, but they cannot participate in all local affairs due to the separation of counties, which is not as good as the taxpayers in the foreign concessions of Shanghai, who still have the right to make suggestions. This is especially fundamentally unsuitable for separation. I have been entrusted by the elders of my hometown to travel and appeal for many years, but the matter has not been resolved. I am restless at night, ashamed beyond measure. I deeply hope that you will examine the people's plight, not be swayed by superficial words, and inform us of the reasons why the Civil Affairs Bureau's submission is irreversible, so that we can consider and restore our reputation. You love the people of Jiangsu and treat them equally, and you should not neglect Chongming and Qidong because they are remote. Wang Qingmu, October 31st."

Wang Chengying Returned to Hangzhou to Report that the Zhejiang Province Loan Negotiation Was Concluded 132

5 Million Debt Tickets Pledged at 60% Discount with Monthly Interest of 8%

Will Bring the Contract to Shanghai for Signing as Soon as the Draft is Completed

Wang Chengying, Director of the Finance Department of Zhejiang Province, has been negotiating for a loan of 20 million yuan secured by local public debt tickets of the province in the 23rd year of the Republic. Since March 10th, he has invited the leaders of various banks for discussions several times, and an agreement has been reached. A loan of 3 million yuan will be secured by public debt tickets with a face value of 5 million yuan at a 60% discount for the purpose of handling the small winter relief and public security expenses. The monthly interest rate is 8%, and the loan will be repaid in two years. All conditions will be handled in accordance with the Jiangsu Public Debt method. The borrowing banks are China, Communications, Shanghai, Zhongnan, Zhejiang Industrial, Zhejiang Real Estate, China Real Estate, Siming, Jincheng, Jianye, Continental, and Commercial banks, etc., twelve banks in total. The amount of the loan undertaken by each bank has also been allocated. As for the loan contract, the manager of the Zhejiang Local Bank returned to Hangzhou from Shanghai on the 18th to draft it, referring to the old loan contract of the Zhejiang Provincial Government. Director Wang originally planned to stay in Shanghai to wait for the signing, but because the affairs of the Finance Department are cumbersome and need to be dealt with urgently, he took the Shanghai-Hangzhou train back to Hangzhou at 6:50 pm on the 21st to report the negotiation process to the provincial government meeting and discuss the issuance procedures. As soon as the contract is drafted, he will bring the contract to Shanghai and invite all the borrowing banks to formally sign it.

Alcohol Consolidated Tax to be Levied Today 133

Tax Administration Announces Regulations

The Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance announced today the [Provisional Regulations for Alcohol Consolidated Tax], which will be levied from today. The [Collection Regulations] are also announced at the same time. The main points are as follows:

Types of Alcohol: All alcohol manufactured domestically or imported from abroad will be subject to consolidated tax. When imported goods enter the country, import duties will still be paid first, but after the consolidated tax has been levied, no further taxes will be levied when the goods are sold in various provinces.

Two Tax Rates: Alcohol is divided into two categories, A and B, for taxation. A: Ordinary alcohol, the tax rate is 1 jiao and 3 fen per liter in national currency. B: Denatured alcohol and wood alcohol (including light coconut wine and fusel oil), 6 fen and 5 li per liter. Regardless of whether it is in barrels or packages, the tax should be calculated based on the net volume of each barrel or package. Any fraction of a liter less than one liter will be counted as one liter. For boxed items, the volume of each item in the box should be calculated. Any remainder less than one liter will also be counted as one liter. For bottled items that are not in boxes, each bottle should be counted. The method is the same as above.

Collection Method: For domestically produced alcohol, tax officials will be stationed at the factory to collect the tax. For alcohol imported from abroad, the customs will collect the tax at the same time when the goods are unloaded from the warehouse and import duties are paid. A passport should be obtained for transportation to other ports.

Tax Refund Method: If alcohol that has already paid consolidated tax is sold in various provinces and is re-taxed, evidence should be submitted within three months to request a tax refund from the original consolidated tax agency. If domestically produced alcohol is sold overseas, or imported alcohol is re-exported domestically, a tax refund can also be obtained according to legal procedures. Inspection and Registration: Manufacturers of alcohol should report the start time of work, and resident staff will supervise. When starting transportation, transferring, and arriving, reports should also be submitted for inspection. New alcohol factories must report to the local tax authorities three weeks before starting production and submit it to the Tax Administration for registration. They must also register with the Trademark Bureau first, and only after registration and approval can they select a brand name.

Punishment Method: If a manufacturer or dealer commits one of the following acts, in addition to confiscating the tax-evaded alcohol, a fine of up to ten times the amount of tax evaded will be imposed, and those who violate criminal law will be transferred to the judicial authorities for investigation. 1. Transporting and selling alcohol without affixing stamps or obtaining transport permits in accordance with regulations. 2. Privately manufacturing alcohol and secretly transporting it out of the factory for sale. 3. Counterfeiting the trademarks of other companies, privately manufacturing alcohol, and selling it on the market to evade taxes. 4. Counterfeiting stamps, documents, seals, or using counterfeit stamps and documents to evade taxes. 5. Reusing old stamps, or reusing old boxes and barrels without checking the stamps, and reloading them for sale. 6. Discrepancies between goods and documents, or having goods without documents, which is found to be tax evasion. 7. The number of alcohol in the factory stock does not match the records, and it is proven to be evasion. 8. The amount of stamps affixed is insufficient. 9. Reporting ordinary alcohol as denatured alcohol to reduce the tax rate. In addition, alcohol manufacturers or dealers who commit one of the following acts will be fined up to 200 yuan, depending on the circumstances: (1) Tearing off old stamps that have been affixed in preparation for reuse, and there is evidence to prove it. 2. Privately transporting alcohol containers with old stamps that have not been washed into the alcohol factory without the supervision of the resident staff, and privately manufacturing alcohol. The privately manufactured alcohol will be confiscated.

Municipal Residents Advocate the National Goods Association to Prepare for the Shanghai West National Goods Exhibition 134

Registration Started Yesterday

Opening on December 1st

The Shanghai Municipal Residents National Goods Promotion Association held a national goods exhibition for three weeks in the winter of the 21st year of the Republic of China. To expand the promotion of national goods and complete the national goods movement, the 19th Standing Committee meeting of the 14th session decided to hold the Second Shanghai West National Goods Exhibition. All preparatory work was handed over to the Cooperative Department to be prepared under the responsibility of the Standing Committee member. The Wujiaochang Zhaoji Middle School sports field in the central location of Shanghai West has been selected as the venue. Xu Jianruo, a member of the Standing Committee, designed the venue drawings, and Zheng Zhenghe Construction Company was hired to build it, with a deadline of the 20th of this month. The opening date is set for December 1st. All registration matters are presided over by Xu Yunhui, a member of the Cooperative Department, and are strictly revised. The participating industries are divided into 37 categories, with six companies for each industry's essential goods, three companies for ordinary goods, and one company for marketable goods. The preparation fee budget has been audited by the Finance Department, and the total case is estimated at 3,000 yuan. Each booth for participating factories will be charged a preparation fee of 20 yuan to reduce the burden on each factory. Yesterday, the secretariat sent a notice to all factory members to solicit participation, and registration is scheduled to begin at 2:00 pm on the 23rd (today). Registration will be closed as soon as the quota is full, and it has been reported to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Bureau for record. Letters have also been sent to various agencies and public organizations in Shanghai West to assist in the progress and jointly participate in the event.

Xu Shiying Returns to Shanghai 138

Discusses Completion of Huangshan Construction

Scheduled to Visit Jiang in Nanjing to Report

Mr. Xu Shiying, Chairman of the National Relief Commission, previously traveled to Nanjing with Huang Bodu in secret to attend the Finance Conference of the Huai River Conservancy Commission. Afterwards, he took a car from Nanjing, passing through Wuhu, to Huangshan to inspect the construction projects. Due to the numerous important matters in Shanghai awaiting his attention, and with the imminent opening of the Drought Relief Association meeting, he left Huangshan the day before yesterday and returned to Shanghai. He arrived at the Shanghai Railway Station by express train from Hangzhou at 7:20 PM the day before yesterday, and immediately proceeded to Father Lao's private residence to rest. According to Mr. Xu's statement to a reporter from the China Eastern News Agency yesterday:

"This time, I wanted to personally inspect the disaster situation in rural areas of various counties, and to conveniently inspect the preliminary planning of the three-month construction project on Huangshan. I took the route through Nanjing, Wuhu, Tunxi, and other places. Along the way, I witnessed the extremely severe disaster situation everywhere. The hardship and suffering of the farmers are almost indescribable. In the places I passed, there were only withered rice stalks, barely a foot tall, remaining in the fields. There was almost no straw stacked in the villages and fields. The meager harvest is imaginable. All the counties I passed through in Anhui Province—Wuhu, Xuancheng, Ningguo, Jixi, Shexian, Xiuning—and in Zhejiang Province—Changhua, Yuchangqian, Lin'an, Hangzhou, Haining, Jiashan, Jiaxing—are affected by the disaster. No place is spared, and the disaster is severe everywhere. The farmers have no savings and are completely impoverished. Winter is fast approaching, and I don't know how they will survive. I sincerely hope that people in the country will do their best to provide relief so that they can overcome the difficulties of this year and plan for stability next spring, which would be a blessing for the nation."

"The preliminary construction project on Huangshan has been completed according to the original plan. The total cost of various items is only 16,500 yuan in national currency, which was raised through donations handled by Shiying. The buildings include the Guxiangfu Temple, Jushilin, Bianxi Pavilion, Banshan Temple, Chengxiangyuan, and Yungu Hall. They are generally in line with the principles of simplicity, elegance, firmness, and beauty that I set. The rearrangement of the Front Sea and Back Sea, and the construction of roads and bridges, are also commendable. In addition, the Tangquan and Chishanglou, repaired with funds allocated by the Anhui Provincial Government; the Lansheng Pavilion, donated by Director Liu Shi'an; and the Bailong Bridge, donated by Mr. Li Fanyi, add beauty to the mountain scenery. The two roads opened by Mr. Wu Zhihui through donations to ascend to the peak of Tiandu Peak and to the West Sea Gate are particularly admirable. In such a short period, with such a small amount of money, it was possible to achieve the above results. This is due to the guidance of the provincial authorities, the advocacy of the donors, the support of all parties, and the efforts of the staff stationed on the mountain. I am extremely pleased." Mr. Xu then listed the names of the donors. Those who have already paid include: the Central Relief Commission, with 1,000 yuan for work relief; the Xinwei Relief Association, with 1,000 yuan for work relief; Duan Zhilao, 500 yuan; Mr. Zhang Xiaolin, 1,500 yuan; Mr. Du Yuesheng, 1,500 yuan; Mr. Xu Jingren, 1,500 yuan; Mr. Wang Xiaolai, 1,000 yuan; Chairman Liu Xueya, 1,000 yuan; Mr. Wu Dieqing, 1,000 yuan; Mr. Zhu Douwen and Mr. Zhu Rushan jointly donated 1,000 yuan; Mr. Wang Yiting, 700 yuan; Mr. Wang Zhongqi, 700 yuan; Mr. Bai Liewu, 500 yuan; Mr. Yang Xiaotian, 500 yuan; Mr. Shi Liangcai, 500 yuan; Mr. Liu Xueyuan, 500 yuan; Mr. Chen Chucun, 100 yuan; Mr. Lin Jinwen, 50 yuan; Mr. Hong Yulin and Mr. Huang Bodu jointly donated 150 yuan; Shiying, 200 yuan; Xu Huisui, 200 yuan; Xu Shen Yiren, 100 yuan. There are still those who have pledged but not yet paid, and efforts are being made to collect them. In the future, a list will be published in the newspaper to express gratitude, and a monument will be erected on the mountain to engrave their names. The revenue and expenditure items will be sent to an accountant for audit and public announcement. The head of the technical team stationed on the mountain is Jin Weinong, and the head of the general affairs team is Hou Huizheng, who have worked tirelessly and diligently, and I express my extreme gratitude."

Mr. Xu then briefly described the specific plans for the future construction of Huangshan, saying, "I have some preliminary ideas and have formulated specific plans. The draft implementation plan for the first year is to lease out public land in the Taoyuan area within January and February. The construction work should primarily focus on developing transportation within the mountain. In addition to renovating the main roads in the Front Sea and Back Sea, the roads in the North Sea area should also be greatly repaired to facilitate tourists traveling from Taiping and other counties, so as to achieve balanced development. Public buildings in the various school Yuan Village residential areas and the Ziyunji commercial area, as well as public security, production and construction, geological flora and fauna surveys, and geodetic surveying, also urgently need to be addressed. The protection and restoration of scenic spots and historical sites throughout the mountain, and the promotion and improvement of local specialties, are particularly important, as Huangshan has many specialties, some of which are extremely valuable. The area below the West Sea Gate has been untouched by humans for thousands of years, and I plan to organize an expedition immediately. However, I am only one of the standing members of the Huangshan Construction Committee, and I need to discuss this in detail with Chairman Liu and other standing members before submitting it to the general meeting for deliberation and decision. I sincerely hope that enlightened people across the country will provide more guidance. Not only will this committee be happy to accept it, but it is also what Shiying personally hopes for." Mr. Xu also said that transportation outside Huangshan Mountain is now more convenient than before. The Hangzhou-Hui, Wuhu-Tunxi, and Yin-Tunxi roads have long been open to traffic. Tourists can travel from Hangzhou, Shanghai, Nanjing, Wuhu, Datong, Jiujiang, and other places and arrive in the morning and evening. The order in the surrounding areas is very good. I arrived on the mountain at 4:00 AM on the 11th and had no escorts. The road was very peaceful. The reporter then asked if the chairman, who is sixty-two years old, felt tired climbing the mountain at night. Mr. Xu replied with a smile, "It's not just climbing the mountain at night, but also hiking in the mountains on dark nights for 30 to 50 li (approximately 15 to 25 kilometers) every day. This is because the scenery of Huangshan is magnificent, majestic, secluded, and beautiful, and it is enough to please the heart and mind. I remember climbing Bihai to Believe Peak on the 16th and seeing Jiuhua Mountain and Lushan Mountain as clearly as if they were painted. The white clouds on the river were like strips of silk. Then I went to the West Sea Gate and looked at the peaks of the West Sea. I marveled at the wonders of nature, the work of ghosts and gods, which is unbelievable. Therefore, each visit is a new discovery. I enjoy this and don't get tired of it. People say that the scenery of Huangshan is unique in the world, and the joy of traveling in Huangshan is unparalleled. Those who have visited will not think this is an exaggeration. There is a couplet in Lion Forest that says, 'So wonderful that it cannot be described, how could this be? Those who arrive will know.' You cannot understand the recording without experiencing it yourself." According to Mr. Xu's aides, Chairman Jiang is very concerned about relief work and the construction of Huangshan when he is in Nanjing. President Wang is also concerned about Huangshan. Xu plans to visit Nanjing in a few days after resting to seek instructions.
